## Proof of sub-idR

The proof of `sub-idR` follows directly from `sub-id`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="sub-idR"></a><a id="17719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17719" class="Function">sub-idR</a> <a id="17727" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17729" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="17731" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17731" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="17733" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17733" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="17734" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17736" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17737" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17737" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="17739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17741" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2460" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="17747" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17731" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="17749" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17733" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="17750" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17752" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17753" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17753" class="Bound">A</a><a id="17754" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="17763" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17765" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17766" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17737" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="17768" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3815" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="17770" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3101" class="Function">ids</a><a id="17773" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17775" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="17777" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17737" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="17779" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17780" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17753" class="Bound">A</a><a id="17781" class="Symbol">}</a>
<a id="17783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17719" class="Function">sub-idR</a> <a id="17791" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17792" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17792" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="17793" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17795" class="Argument">σ</a> <a id="17797" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17799" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17799" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="17800" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17802" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17802" class="Bound">A</a><a id="17803" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17805" class="Symbol">=</a>
          <a id="17817" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2597" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
            <a id="17835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17799" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="17837" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3815" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="17839" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3101" class="Function">ids</a>
          <a id="17853" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
            <a id="17869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="17871" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3101" class="Function">ids</a> <a id="17875" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="17877" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="17879" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17799" class="Bound">σ</a>
          <a id="17891" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="17894" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#1982" class="Postulate">extensionality</a> <a id="17909" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="17912" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17912" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17914" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17916" href="plfa.Substitution.html#17041" class="Function">sub-id</a><a id="17922" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17924" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
            <a id="17938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#17799" class="Bound">σ</a>
          <a id="17950" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

## Proof of sub-sub

The `sub-sub` equation states that sequenced substitutions `σ ⨟ τ`
are equivalent to first applying `σ` then applying `τ`.

    ⟪ τ ⟫ ⟪ σ ⟫ M  ≡ ⟪ σ ⨟ τ ⟫ M

The proof requires several lemmas. First, we need to prove the
specialization for renaming.

    rename ρ (rename ρ′ M) ≡ rename (ρ ∘ ρ′) M

This in turn requires the following lemma about `ext`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="compose-ext"></a><a id="18338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18338" class="Function">compose-ext</a> <a id="18350" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18352" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="18354" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18354" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18356" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18356" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="18358" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18358" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="18359" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18361" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18361" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18363" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18365" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="18372" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18356" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="18374" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18358" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="18375" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18377" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18378" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18378" class="Bound">ρ′</a> <a id="18381" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18383" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="18390" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18354" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18392" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18356" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="18393" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18395" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18396" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18396" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18398" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18398" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18399" class="Symbol">}</a>
            <a id="18413" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18415" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="18417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18361" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="18422" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18424" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18427" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18431" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18378" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18433" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18436" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18438" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18442" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18443" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18361" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18445" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18447" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18378" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18449" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18451" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18452" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18398" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18453" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18456" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18396" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18457" class="Symbol">}</a>
<a id="18459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18338" class="Function">compose-ext</a> <a id="18471" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18473" href="plfa.Substitution.html#1982" class="Postulate">extensionality</a> <a id="18488" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18490" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18490" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18494" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18518" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="18500" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18501" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="18503" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18505" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18490" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18506" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="18510" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="18518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18518" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="18524" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18526" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="18528" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18528" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18530" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18530" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="18532" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18532" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="18533" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18535" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18535" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18539" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="18546" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18530" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="18548" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18532" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="18549" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18551" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18552" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18552" class="Bound">ρ′</a> <a id="18555" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18557" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="18564" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18528" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18566" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18530" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="18567" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18569" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18570" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18570" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18572" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18572" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18573" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18575" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18576" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18576" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18578" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18580" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18528" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18584" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18572" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18586" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3483" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="18588" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18570" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18589" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="18605" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18607" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="18609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18535" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="18614" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18616" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18619" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18623" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18552" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18625" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18628" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18576" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18630" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18632" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="18636" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18637" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18535" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18639" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="18641" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18552" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="18643" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18645" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18576" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="18649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18518" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="18655" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18656" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="18658" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3519" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a><a id="18661" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18663" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18665" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
  <a id="18672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18518" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="18678" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18679" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="18681" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="18685" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18685" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18686" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18688" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18690" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
To prove that composing renamings is equivalent to applying one after
the other using `rename`, we proceed by induction on the term `M`,
using the `compose-ext` lemma in the case for `M ≡ ƛ N`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="compose-rename"></a><a id="18899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="18914" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18916" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="18918" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18918" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18920" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18920" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="18922" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18922" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="18923" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18925" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18925" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18926" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18928" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18928" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="18930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18932" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18918" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="18936" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18925" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18937" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18939" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18939" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18943" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="18950" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18920" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="18952" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18922" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="18953" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18955" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18955" class="Bound">ρ′</a> <a id="18958" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18960" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="18967" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18918" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="18969" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18920" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="18970" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="18974" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="18983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18939" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="18985" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18986" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="18993" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18955" class="Bound">ρ′</a> <a id="18996" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18928" class="Bound">M</a><a id="18997" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18999" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="19001" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="19008" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19009" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18939" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19011" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="19013" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18955" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19015" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19017" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18928" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="19019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="19034" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19035" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="19037" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4288" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="19041" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19041" class="Bound">x</a><a id="19042" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19044" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19046" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
<a id="19051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="19066" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19067" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19067" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19068" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19070" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19070" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="19071" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19073" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19073" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="19074" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19076" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19076" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19077" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="19081" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19081" class="Bound">N</a><a id="19082" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19084" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19084" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="19085" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19087" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19087" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19089" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19091" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19093" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1090" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="19098" href="plfa.Untyped.html#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="19101" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19113" class="Function">G</a>
  <a id="19105" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="19113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19113" class="Function">G</a> <a id="19115" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="19124" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19125" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19129" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19084" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="19130" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19132" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19133" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="19140" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19141" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19145" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19087" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19147" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19149" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19081" class="Bound">N</a><a id="19150" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19152" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="19154" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="19161" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19162" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19166" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19167" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19084" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19169" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="19171" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19087" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19173" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19176" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19081" class="Bound">N</a>

      <a id="19245" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="19248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a><a id="19262" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19263" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="19265" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19271" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19084" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="19272" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19274" class="Argument">ρ′</a> <a id="19277" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19279" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19283" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19087" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19285" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19287" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
        <a id="19297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="19304" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="19306" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19084" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="19311" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19313" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="19315" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19316" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19320" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19087" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19322" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19325" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19081" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="19333" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="19336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#10425" class="Function">cong-rename</a> <a id="19348" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18338" class="Function">compose-ext</a> <a id="19360" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="19365" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
        <a id="19375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="19382" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19383" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="19387" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19388" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19084" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19390" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="19392" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19087" class="Bound">ρ′</a><a id="19394" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19397" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19081" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="19405" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
<a id="19407" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="19422" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19423" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="19425" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19427" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19427" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="19429" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4400" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="19431" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19431" class="Bound">M</a><a id="19432" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19434" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19436" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1436" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="19442" href="plfa.Untyped.html#4400" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="19446" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="19461" href="plfa.Substitution.html#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The next lemma states that if a renaming and substitution commute on
variables, then they also commute on terms. We explain the proof in
detail below.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="commute-subst-rename"></a><a id="19637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19637" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a> <a id="19658" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19660" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="19662" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19662" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19664" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19664" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="19665" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19667" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19667" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="19669" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19671" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19662" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19675" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="19676" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19678" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19678" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="19680" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19682" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2460" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="19688" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19662" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19690" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19664" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="19691" class="Symbol">}</a>
                        <a id="19717" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19718" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19720" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19722" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="19724" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19724" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19725" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19727" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19729" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="19736" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19724" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19738" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19739" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19724" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="19743" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="19744" class="Symbol">)}</a>
     <a id="19752" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19754" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="19757" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19757" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19759" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19761" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19662" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19763" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3483" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="19765" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="19766" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19768" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19770" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="19775" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19678" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="19777" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19778" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="19780" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19782" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="19783" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19785" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19786" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19718" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19788" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19757" class="Bound">x</a><a id="19789" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19791" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="19793" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="19800" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19718" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="19802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19803" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19678" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="19805" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19757" class="Bound">x</a><a id="19806" class="Symbol">))</a>

     <a id="20333" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="20336" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1090" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="20341" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20342" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="20349" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a><a id="20351" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19950" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="20355" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>

     <a id="20396" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="20399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="20414" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>

     <a id="20450" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="20453" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#10425" class="Function">cong-rename</a> <a id="20465" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="20470" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="20475" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
       <a id="20484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="20491" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="20493" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="20497" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19947" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20498" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20500" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="20502" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a><a id="20504" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20507" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19944" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="20509" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20236" class="Bound">y</a><a id="20510" class="Symbol">)</a>
     <a id="20517" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="20520" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#939" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="20524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#18899" class="Function">compose-rename</a> <a id="20539" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>

       <a id="20597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="20604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20605" href="plfa.Untyped.html#5883" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="20609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19947" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20610" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20613" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="20618" href="plfa.Substitution.html#19944" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="20620" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20621" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="20623" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20236" class="Bound">y</a><a id="20624" class="Symbol">))</a>
     <a id="20632" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
<a id="20634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19637" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a> <a id="20655" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20656" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="20658" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20660" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20660" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="20662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4400" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="20664" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20664" class="Bound">M</a><a id="20665" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20667" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="20669" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20671" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20671" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20672" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20674" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20674" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="20676" class="Symbol">=</a>
   <a id="20681" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1436" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="20687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4400" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="20691" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19637" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a><a id="20712" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20713" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="20715" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20717" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20660" class="Bound">L</a><a id="20718" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20720" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="20722" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20724" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20671" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20725" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20727" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20674" class="Bound">r</a><a id="20728" class="Symbol">)</a>
             <a id="20743" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19637" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a><a id="20764" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20765" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="20767" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20769" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20664" class="Bound">M</a><a id="20770" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20772" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="20774" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20776" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20671" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="20777" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20779" href="plfa.Substitution.html#20674" class="Bound">r</a><a id="20780" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The proof is by induction on the term `M`.

* If `M` is a variable, then we use the premise to conclude.

* If `M ≡ ƛ N`, we conclude using the induction hypothesis for
  `N`. However, to use the induction hypothesis, we must show
  that

        exts (exts σ) (ext ρ x) ≡ rename (ext ρ) (exts σ x)

  We prove this equation by cases on x.

    * If `x = Z`, the two sides are equal by definition.

    * If `x = S y`, we obtain the goal by the following equational reasoning.

          exts (exts σ) (ext ρ (S y))
        ≡ rename S_ (exts σ (ρ y))
        ≡ rename S_ (rename S_ (σ (ρ y)      (by the premise)
        ≡ rename (ext ρ) (exts σ (S y))      (by compose-rename)
        ≡ rename ((ext ρ) ∘ S_) (σ y)
        ≡ rename (ext ρ) (rename S_ (σ y))   (by compose-rename)
        ≡ rename (ext ρ) (exts σ (S y))

* If `M` is an application, we obtain the goal using the induction
  hypothesis for each subterm.


The last lemma needed to prove `sub-sub` states that the `exts`
function distributes with sequencing. It is a corollary of
`commute-subst-rename` as described below.  (It would have been nicer
to prove this directly by equational reasoning in the σ algebra, but
that would require the `sub-assoc` equation, whose proof depends on
`sub-sub`, which in turn depends on this lemma.)

     <a id="22490" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
       <a id="22501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="22503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="22508" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22435" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="22511" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="22513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22514" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="22521" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="22524" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22525" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22431" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22528" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22428" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22529" class="Symbol">))</a>
     <a id="22537" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="22540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#19637" class="Function">commute-subst-rename</a><a id="22560" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22561" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="22563" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22565" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22431" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22568" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22428" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22569" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="22571" class="Argument">σ</a> <a id="22573" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22575" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22435" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="22577" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="22579" class="Argument">ρ</a> <a id="22581" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a><a id="22585" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22587" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="22592" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
       <a id="22601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="22608" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="22611" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="22614" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22435" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="22617" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="22619" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22620" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22431" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22623" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22428" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22624" class="Symbol">))</a>
     <a id="22632" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
       <a id="22643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="22650" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a> <a id="22653" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="22655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#22431" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="22658" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3815" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="22660" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22435" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="22662" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22664" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22428" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22665" class="Symbol">)</a>
     <a id="22672" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The proof proceed by cases on `x`.

* If `x = Z`, the two sides are equal by the definition of `exts`
  and sequencing.

* If `x = S x`, we unfold the first use of `exts` and sequencing, then
  apply the lemma `commute-subst-rename`. We conclude by the
  definition of sequencing.


Now we come to the proof of `sub-sub`, which we explain below.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="sub-sub"></a><a id="23030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#23030" class="Function">sub-sub</a> <a id="23038" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23040" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="23042" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23042" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="23044" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23044" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="23046" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23046" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="23047" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23049" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23049" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23050" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23052" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23052" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="23054" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23056" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23042" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="23058" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="23060" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23049" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23061" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23063" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23064" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23064" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="23067" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23069" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2460" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="23075" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23042" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="23077" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23044" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="23078" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23080" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23080" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="23083" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23085" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2460" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="23091" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23044" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="23093" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23046" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="23094" class="Symbol">}</a>
            <a id="23108" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23112" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23080" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="23115" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23117" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23118" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23120" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23064" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="23123" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23125" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23052" class="Bound">M</a><a id="23126" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23128" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="23130" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23132" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23064" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="23135" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3815" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="23137" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23080" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="23140" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23142" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23052" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="23144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#23030" class="Function">sub-sub</a> <a id="23152" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23153" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="23155" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4288" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="23159" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23159" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23160" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23162" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23164" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
<a id="23169" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#23030" class="Function">sub-sub</a> <a id="23177" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23178" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23178" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="23179" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23181" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23181" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="23182" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23184" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23184" class="Bound">Σ</a><a id="23185" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23187" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23187" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23188" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23190" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="23192" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23192" class="Bound">N</a><a id="23193" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23195" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23195" class="Bound">σ₁</a><a id="23197" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23199" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23199" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="23201" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23203" class="Symbol">=</a>
   <a id="23208" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2597" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
     <a id="23219" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23221" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23199" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="23224" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23226" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23227" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23229" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23195" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="23232" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23234" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="23237" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23192" class="Bound">N</a><a id="23238" class="Symbol">))</a>
   <a id="23244" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2655" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
     <a id="23253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="23255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23257" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="23262" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23199" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="23265" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23267" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23268" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23270" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="23275" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23195" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="23278" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23280" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23192" class="Bound">N</a><a id="23281" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="23286" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="23289" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1090" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="23294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="23297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#23030" class="Function">sub-sub</a><a id="23305" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23306" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="23308" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23310" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23192" class="Bound">N</a><a id="23311" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23313" class="Argument">σ₁</a> <a id="23316" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23318" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="23323" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23195" class="Bound">σ₁</a><a id="23325" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23327" class="Argument">σ₂</a> <a id="23330" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23332" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="23337" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23199" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="23339" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="23342" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="23349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="23351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23353" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="23358" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23195" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="23361" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3815" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="23363" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="23368" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23199" class="Bound">σ₂</a> <a id="23371" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23373" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23192" class="Bound">N</a>
   <a id="23378" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">≡⟨</a> <a id="23381" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1090" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="23386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="23389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23390" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#11227" class="Function">cong-sub</a><a id="23398" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23399" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="23401" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23403" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23192" class="Bound">N</a><a id="23404" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23406" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="23409" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23410" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23410" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23411" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23413" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23415" href="plfa.Substitution.html#22093" class="Function">exts-seq</a><a id="23423" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23425" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="23429" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23431" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2714" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="23438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="23440" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="23442" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="23447" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23449" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23195" class="Bound">σ₁</a> <a id="23452" href="plfa.Substitution.html#3815" class="Function Operator">⨟</a> <a id="23454" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23199" class="Bound">σ₂</a><a id="23456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23458" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="23460" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23192" class="Bound">N</a>
   <a id="23465" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
<a id="23467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#23030" class="Function">sub-sub</a> <a id="23475" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23476" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="23478" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23480" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23480" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="23482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4400" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="23484" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23484" class="Bound">M</a><a id="23485" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23487" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23489" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1436" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="23495" href="plfa.Untyped.html#4400" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="23499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23500" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23030" class="Function">sub-sub</a><a id="23507" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23508" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="23510" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23512" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23480" class="Bound">L</a><a id="23513" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="23516" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23517" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23030" class="Function">sub-sub</a><a id="23524" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23525" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="23527" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23529" href="plfa.Substitution.html#23484" class="Bound">M</a><a id="23530" class="Symbol">})</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
We proceed by induction on the term `M`.

* If `M = x`, then both sides are equal to `σ₂ (σ₁ x)`.

* If `M = ƛ N`, we first use the induction hypothesis to show that

     ƛ ⟪ exts σ₂ ⟫ (⟪ exts σ₁ ⟫ N) ≡ ƛ ⟪ exts σ₁ ⨟ exts σ₂ ⟫ N

  and then use the lemma `exts-seq` to show

    ƛ ⟪ exts σ₁ ⨟ exts σ₂ ⟫ N ≡ ƛ ⟪ exts ( σ₁ ⨟ σ₂) ⟫ N

* If `M` is an application, we use the induction hypothesis
  for both subterms.


The following corollary of `sub-sub` specializes the first
substitution to a renaming.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="rename-subst"></a><a id="24046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#24046" class="Function">rename-subst</a> <a id="24059" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24061" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24063" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24063" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24065" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24065" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="24067" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24067" class="Bound">Δ′</a><a id="24069" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24071" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24071" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="24073" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24075" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24063" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="24079" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="24080" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24082" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24082" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24084" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24086" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2247" class="Function">Rename</a> <a id="24093" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24063" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24095" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24065" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="24096" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24098" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24098" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="24100" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24102" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2460" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="24108" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24065" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="24110" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24067" class="Bound">Δ′</a><a id="24112" class="Symbol">}</a>
             <a id="24127" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="24131" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24098" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="24133" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="24135" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6193" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="24143" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24082" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24145" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24071" class="Bound">M</a><a id="24146" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24148" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="24150" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="24152" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24098" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="24154" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Function.html#1099" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="24156" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24082" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24158" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="24160" href="plfa.Substitution.html#24071" class="Bound">M</a>

## Proof of sub-assoc

The proof of `sub-assoc` follows directly from `sub-sub` and the
definition of sequencing.

## Proof of subst-zero-exts-cons

The last equation we needed to prove `subst-zero-exts-cons` was
`sub-assoc`, so we can now go ahead with its proof.  We simply apply
the equations for `exts` and `subst-zero` and then apply the σ algebra
equation to arrive at the normal form `M • σ`.

</pre>{% endraw %}

## Proof of the substitution lemma

We first prove the generalized form of the substitution lemma, showing
that a substitution `σ` commutes with the substitution of `M` into
`N`.

    ⟪ exts σ ⟫ N [ ⟪ σ ⟫ M ] ≡ ⟪ σ ⟫ (N [ M ])

This proof is where the σ algebra pays off.  The proof is by direct
equational reasoning. Starting with the left-hand side, we apply σ
algebra equations, oriented left-to-right, until we arrive at the
normal form

    ⟪ ⟪ σ ⟫ M • σ ⟫ N

We then do the same with the right-hand side, arriving at the same
normal form.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="subst-commute"></a><a id="26467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26467" class="Function">subst-commute</a> <a id="26481" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26483" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="26485" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26485" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26487" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26487" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="26488" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26490" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26490" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="26492" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26494" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26485" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26496" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26498" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="26500" href="plfa.Untyped.html#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="26502" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="26503" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26505" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26505" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="26507" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26509" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26485" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26511" href="plfa.Untyped.html#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="26513" href="plfa.Untyped.html#2876" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="26514" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26516" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26516" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="26518" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26520" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2460" class="Function">Subst</a> <a id="26526" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26485" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26528" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26487" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="26530" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="26536" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="26540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="26545" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26516" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="26547" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="26549" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26490" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="26551" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7449" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="26553" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="26555" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26516" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="26557" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="26559" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26505" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="26561" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7449" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="26563" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="26565" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="26567" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26516" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="26569" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="26571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26572" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26490" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="26574" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7449" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="26576" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26505" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="26578" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7449" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="26579" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="26581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#26467" class="Function">subst-commute</a> <a id="26595" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26596" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26596" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26597" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26599" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26599" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="26600" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26602" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26602" class="Bound">N</a><a id="26603" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26605" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26605" class="Bound">M</a><a id="26606" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="26608" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26608" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="26609" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26611" class="Symbol">=</a>
     <a id="26618" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2597" class="Function Operator">begin</a>

       <a id="27747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#2601" class="Function Operator">⟪</a> <a id="27749" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26608" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="27751" href="plfa.Substitution.html#2601" class="Function Operator">⟫</a> <a id="27753" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27754" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26602" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="27756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#7449" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="27758" href="plfa.Substitution.html#26605" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="27760" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7449" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="27761" class="Symbol">)</a>
     <a id="27768" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
A corollary of `subst-commute` is that `rename` also commutes with
substitution. In the proof below, we first exchange `rename ρ` for
the substitution `⟪ ren ρ ⟫`, and apply `subst-commute`, and
then convert back to `rename ρ`.

       <a id="28517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6921" class="Function">subst</a> <a id="28523" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#6553" class="Function">ren</a> <a id="28528" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28176" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="28529" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28531" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28532" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28170" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="28534" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7449" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="28536" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28173" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="28538" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7449" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="28539" class="Symbol">)</a>

     <a id="28605" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2892" class="Function Operator">∎</a>

To present the substitution lemma, we introduce the following notation
for substituting a term `M` for index 1 within term `N`.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_〔_〕"></a><a id="28745" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28745" class="Function Operator">_〔_〕</a> <a id="28750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28752" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="28754" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28755" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28755" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28757" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28757" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28759" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28759" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28761" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28761" class="Bound">C</a><a id="28762" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="28772" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28755" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28778" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28759" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28780" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28782" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28761" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="28784" href="plfa.Untyped.html#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="28786" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28757" class="Bound">A</a>
        <a id="28796" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28755" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="28802" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28759" class="Bound">B</a>
          <a id="28814" class="Comment">---------</a>
        <a id="28832" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28755" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28838" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28761" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="28840" href="plfa.Untyped.html#4252" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="28842" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28757" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="28844" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28745" class="Function Operator">_〔_〕</a> <a id="28849" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28850" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28850" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="28851" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28853" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28854" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28854" class="Bound">A</a><a id="28855" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28857" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28858" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28858" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28859" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28861" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28862" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28862" class="Bound">C</a><a id="28863" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28865" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28865" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="28867" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28867" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="28869" class="Symbol">=</a>
   <a id="28874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#6921" class="Function">subst</a> <a id="28880" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28881" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Substitution.md %}{% raw %}#28850" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28883" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28885" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28858" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28887" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28889" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28862" class="Bound">C</a><a id="28890" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28892" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28893" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28850" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28895" href="plfa.Untyped.html#3168" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28897" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28862" class="Bound">C</a><a id="28898" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28900" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28901" href="plfa.Untyped.html#6629" class="Function">exts</a> <a id="28906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28907" href="plfa.Untyped.html#7333" class="Function">subst-zero</a> <a id="28918" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28867" class="Bound">M</a><a id="28919" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28922" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28923" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28854" class="Bound">A</a><a id="28924" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28926" href="plfa.Substitution.html#28865" class="Bound">N</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The substitution lemma is stated as follows and proved as a corollary
of the `subst-commute` lemma.

## Notes

Most of the properties and proofs in this file are based on the paper
_Autosubst: Reasoning with de Bruijn Terms and Parallel Substitution_
by Schafer, Tebbi, and Smolka (ITP 2015). That paper, in turn, is
based on the paper of Abadi, Cardelli, Curien, and Levy (1991) that
defines the σ algebra.

This chapter uses the following unicode:

    ⟪  U+27EA  MATHEMATICAL LEFT DOUBLE ANGLE BRACKET (\<<)
    ⟫  U+27EA  MATHEMATICAL RIGHT DOUBLE ANGLE BRACKET (\>>)
    ↑  U+2191  UPWARDS ARROW (\u)
    •  U+2022  BULLET (\bub)
    ⨟  U+2A1F  Z NOTATION SCHEMA COMPOSITION (C-x 8 RET Z NOTATION SCHEMA COMPOSITION)
    〔  U+3014  LEFT TORTOISE SHELL BRACKET (\( option 9 on page 2)
    〕  U+3015  RIGHT TORTOISE SHELL BRACKET (\) option 9 on page 2)
